
fs.state[0].total_flow_balance
fs.state[0].flow_mol_phase[Liq] + fs.state[0].flow_mol_phase[Vap]  ==  fs.state[0].flow_mol

fs.state[0].component_flow_balances[argon]
fs.state[0].flow_mol*fs.state[0].mole_frac_comp[argon]  ==  fs.state[0].flow_mol_phase[Liq]*fs.state[0].mole_frac_phase_comp[Liq,argon] + fs.state[0].flow_mol_phase[Vap]*fs.state[0].mole_frac_phase_comp[Vap,argon]

fs.state[0].component_flow_balances[oxygen]
fs.state[0].flow_mol*fs.state[0].mole_frac_comp[oxygen]  ==  fs.state[0].flow_mol_phase[Liq]*fs.state[0].mole_frac_phase_comp[Liq,oxygen] + fs.state[0].flow_mol_phase[Vap]*fs.state[0].mole_frac_phase_comp[Vap,oxygen]

fs.state[0].component_flow_balances[nitrogen]
fs.state[0].flow_mol*fs.state[0].mole_frac_comp[nitrogen]  ==  fs.state[0].flow_mol_phase[Liq]*fs.state[0].mole_frac_phase_comp[Liq,nitrogen] + fs.state[0].flow_mol_phase[Vap]*fs.state[0].mole_frac_phase_comp[Vap,nitrogen]

fs.state[0].sum_mole_frac
fs.state[0].mole_frac_phase_comp[Liq,argon] + fs.state[0].mole_frac_phase_comp[Liq,oxygen] + fs.state[0].mole_frac_phase_comp[Liq,nitrogen] - (fs.state[0].mole_frac_phase_comp[Vap,argon] + fs.state[0].mole_frac_phase_comp[Vap,oxygen] + fs.state[0].mole_frac_phase_comp[Vap,nitrogen])  ==  0

fs.state[0].phase_fraction_constraint[Liq]
fs.state[0].phase_frac[Liq]*fs.state[0].flow_mol  ==  fs.state[0].flow_mol_phase[Liq]

fs.state[0].phase_fraction_constraint[Vap]
fs.state[0].phase_frac[Vap]*fs.state[0].flow_mol  ==  fs.state[0].flow_mol_phase[Vap]

fs.state[0]._teq_constraint_Vap_Liq
fs.state[0]._teq[Vap,Liq] - fs.state[0].temperature - fs.state[0].s_Vap_Liq[Vap] + fs.state[0].s_Vap_Liq[Liq]  ==  0

fs.state[0].temperature_slack_complementarity_Vap_Liq[Vap]
0.5*(mol/s/K*fs.state[0].s_Vap_Liq[Vap] + fs.state[0].flow_mol_phase[Vap] - ((mol/s/K*fs.state[0].s_Vap_Liq[Vap] - fs.state[0].flow_mol_phase[Vap])**2 + fs.state[0].eps_t_Vap_Liq**2)**0.5)  ==  0

fs.state[0].temperature_slack_complementarity_Vap_Liq[Liq]
0.5*(mol/s/K*fs.state[0].s_Vap_Liq[Liq] + fs.state[0].flow_mol_phase[Liq] - ((mol/s/K*fs.state[0].s_Vap_Liq[Liq] - fs.state[0].flow_mol_phase[Liq])**2 + fs.state[0].eps_t_Vap_Liq**2)**0.5)  ==  0
